name:F‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçy‚Äçi‚Äçj‚Äçi‚Äçu
info:Superior Business Single Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted February 16, 2024
msg:I came here during the Spring Festival and originally planned to stay in Yuzhong, but the all-season chain stores in Yuzhong cost RMB 700 to RMB 800 without breakfast. The better ones were basically RMB 1,000+. I was considering driving myself and taking my children to Super Wings Theme Park, and I have requirements for breakfast. , the environment must be absolutely clean and not noisy, so among many hotels, I finally chose the well-established hotel Wellington, halfway between Happy Valley and Yuzhong. After checking in, I was not disappointed. I originally only booked for 2 nights, but finally decided to extend my stay for one more night. Although the hotel is a bit old, and there are some traces of time in some small corners of the room, the advantages are that the room is very clean, the space is relatively large, the service attitude is very good, there are welcome fruits, and good night milk is given when renewing the subscription, and breakfast is also Satisfies needs (if you have a baby, you must have breakfast, which is convenient). Most importantly, the hotel is independent and has its own area, which is quiet and safe. The room was warm and the children's socks washed at night were dry the next morning. The only drawback is that it is a bit far from the subway and light rail. However, considering that it is very tiring after a day of playing with children and driving in Chongqing is easy to be blurred by electronic eyes and dizzy, the main way to travel is to take a taxi, so the overall feeling of staying here is quite good. Recommended, especially during the Chinese New Year and holidays, it is absolutely cost-effective.
